data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="overall-explanation">In Koa.js, middleware is executed in a more modern and efficient manner, using assertions.</div></div></div></div><div class="result-pane--question-related-fields--c3m--"><div class="overall-explanation-pane--overall-explanation--G-hLQ ud-form-group"><label class="ud-heading-md ud-form-label ud-heading-sm" for="form-group--1303">Overall explanation</label><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:rich-text-viewer:html" class="ud-text-md rt-scaffolding" id="overall-explanation">Mocha relies on external libraries like Chai for assertions, giving developers flexibility. Jest, on the other hand, comes with its built-in expect library, streamlining the testing setup. The combination of Mocha and Chai or Jest and expect is a common choice in Node.js testing.</div></div><div data-purpose="domain-pane" class="domain-pane--domain-pane--Pw9dK"><div class="domain-pane--domain-pane-header--2263m ud-heading-md">Domain</div><div class="ud-text-md">Testing in Node.js (Mocha and Jest)</div></div></div></div></div></div></div>
